<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Text - align</h1>

<h2 id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Text-align-align"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>align</span></strong></h2>

<h3 id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Text-align-Description"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h3>

<p>Controls the placement of the text display.</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=604a60ff-43d6-408a-a16e-ec5fa7056372>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>textObj.align(alignment_constant);</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Text - fitLabel</h1>

<h2 id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Text-fitLabel-fitLabel"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>fitLabel</span></strong></h2>

<h3 id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Text-fitLabel-Description"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h3>

<p>Resizes the box around the widget to fit it to the contents. A padding
argument is optional, to add additional pixels on each side of the text.</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=b46d2bc6-a79f-4353-8d6e-7641fb04a2ac>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>&nbsp;textObj.fitLabel([padding]);</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<p>Note: if a text widget is aligned with Widget.WRAP, fitLabel() will not
alter its width.</p>

style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Parameters</span></strong></h2>

  </td>

  <p>Number of pixels to add to the text box on each side of the text.</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Widget (Base Class)</h1>

<div>

<div>

<p>Desk Phone API features described in this section are deprecated and
supported only on the following models: D40, d45, d50, d60, d62, d65, d70</p>

</div>

</div>

<p>Methods and properties of the Widget object are used to control basic
properties for any UI items. It is not possible to construct a Widget object
directly, but all UI classes and onscreen items inherit their basic
functionality from this Widget base class.&nbsp;</p>

<h3 id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-Methods"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Methods</span></strong></h3>

  object's onFocus handler to be called, which must return true to take focus.</p>
  </td>
 </tr>

  <p>color&nbsp;</p>
  <p>labelColor</p>
  <p>textColor</p>
  </td>
  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>Value for the background color</p>
  <p>Value for the foreground color of all widgets except Input fields</p>
  <p>Value for the foreground color of Input fields</p>
  <p>For D40, D45, D50 and D70 model phones: <strong>white</strong>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<strong>black</strong>.</p>
  <p>For D60, D62, D65 model phones:</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>bgcolor</strong> - main background color (grey 900)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>fgcolor</strong> - main foreground text color (grey
  200)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>titlebgcolor</strong> - title background (blue title
  bar)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>titlefgcolor</strong> - title foreground (white title
  bar text)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>selectbgcolor</strong> - select background (light blue
  select bar)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>selectfgcolor</strong> - select foreground (dark select
  text grey 900)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>modalbgcolor</strong> - dark grey modal background
  (grey 800)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>errorbgcolor</strong> - error background (red)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>errorfgcolor</strong> - error foreground (white text)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>fieldbgcolor</strong> - input field default background
  (light grey 300)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>fieldfgcolor</strong> - input field default foreground
  (dark text grey 900)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>tablfg2color</strong> - table 2 text medium dark grey
  (grey 500)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>tablfg3color</strong> - table 3 text medium light grey
  text (grey 400)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>tablfg4color</strong> - table 4 text red (red 900 also
  matches red softkey)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>tablbdrcolor</strong> - table border color (dark grey
  border lines grey 700)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>skdialcolor</strong> - soft key green dial color (green
  900)</p>
  <p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><strong>skerasecolor</strong> - soft key red delete color (red
  900)</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-top:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>focusable&nbsp;</p>
  </td>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Widget (Base Class) - boxType</h1>

<h1
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-boxType-PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-boxType">Phone
API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Widget (Base Class) - boxType</h1>

<h2 id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-boxType-boxType"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>boxType</span></strong></h2>

<h3
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-boxType-Description"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h3>

<p>Sets the type of box that is drawn around the widget.</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=f42d3ec8-b508-43f6-9e67-0fcb7e286acc>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>var grp = new Group(20, 20, (window.w - 40), (window.h - 40));</pre><pre>window.add(grp);</pre><pre>grp.boxType = Widget.BORDER_BOX;</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<p>NO_BOX draws nothing, and whatever is already on the screen remains.
&nbsp;Other BOX types draw filled images. FRAME types draw non-filled frames;
i.e., the interior is transparent so anything already on the screen typically
can be seen within the frame.</p>

<p>The following illustrations show the various boxType options applied to a
widget defined by &quot;new Group(20, 20, window.w - 40, window.h - 40)&quot;
and containing a single text widget at x=20, y=20:</p>

<div class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'>

<hr size=2 width="100%" align=center>

</div>

<h2
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-boxType-Widget.FLAT_BOX"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Widget.FLAT_BOX</span></strong></h2>

<p>&nbsp;<strong>Widget.FLAT_BOX</strong>&nbsp;is a solid (filled) rectangle
with no border. Here it is shown on a black background.</p>

<div class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'>

<hr size=2 width="100%" align=center>

</div>

<h2
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-boxType-Widget.NO_BOX"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Widget.NO_BOX</span></strong></h2>

<p><strong>Widget.NO_BOX</strong>&nbsp;draws no box. Thus, the background color
shows through the widget as seen in the first example.</p>

<p>The text in the second example is the same color as the background and,
thus. is not visible.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal><img border=0 width=300 height=150 id="Picture 1842515149"
src="Digium%20One%20Page_files/image006.png"></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><img border=0 width=300 height=150 id="Picture 1647007663"
src="Digium%20One%20Page_files/image007.png"></p>

<div class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'>

<hr size=2 width="100%" align=center>

</div>

<h2
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-boxType-Widget.BORDER_BOX"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Widget.BORDER_BOX</span></strong></h2>

<p><strong>Widget.BORDER_BOX</strong>&nbsp;is similar to FLAT_BOX, except the
image is a filled box with a border.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal><img border=0 width=300 height=150 id="Picture 6"
src="Digium%20One%20Page_files/image008.png"></p>

<div class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'>

<hr size=2 width="100%" align=center>

</div>

<h2
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-boxType-Widget.RFLAT_BOX"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Widget.RFLAT_BOX</span></strong>&nbsp;</h2>

<p><strong>Widget.RFLAT_BOX</strong>&nbsp;is a filled box with rounded corners
and no border. Here it is shown on a black background.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal><img border=0 width=300 height=150 id="Picture 8"
src="Digium%20One%20Page_files/image009.png"></p>

<div class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'>

<hr size=2 width="100%" align=center>

</div>

<h2
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-boxType-Widget-ROUNDED_BOX"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Widget-ROUNDED_BOX&nbsp;</span></strong></h2>

<p><strong>Widget-ROUNDED_BOX</strong>&nbsp;is a filled box with a rounded
border.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal><img border=0 width=300 height=150 id="Picture 10"
src="Digium%20One%20Page_files/image010.png"></p>

<div class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'>

<hr size=2 width="100%" align=center>

</div>

<h2
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-boxType-Widget.BORDER_FRAME"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Widget.BORDER_FRAME</span></strong></h2>

<p><strong>Widget.BORDER_FRAME</strong>&nbsp;creates a widget that is a
transparent (non-filled) rectangle with a border. This example shows a group
with its color set to black the background shows through the interior of the
widget.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal><img border=0 width=300 height=150 id="Picture 12"
src="Digium%20One%20Page_files/image011.png"></p>

<div class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'>

<hr size=2 width="100%" align=center>

</div>

<h2
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-boxType-Widget.OVAL_FRAME"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Widget.OVAL_FRAME</span></strong></h2>

<p><strong>Widget.OVAL_FRAME</strong>&nbsp;creates a widget that is a
transparent (non-filled) oval frame with a border.&nbsp;</p>

<p class=MsoNormal><img border=0 width=300 height=150 id="Picture 14"
src="Digium%20One%20Page_files/image012.png"></p>

<div class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'>

<hr size=2 width="100%" align=center>

</div>

<h2
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-boxType-Widget.OVAL_BOX"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Widget.
OVAL_BOX</span></strong></h2>

<p><strong>Widget. OVAL_BOX</strong>&nbsp;is a filled oval shape with a border.</p>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Widget (Base Class) -
onkey[key]</h1>

<h1
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-onkey[key]-PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-onkey[key]">Phone
API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Widget (Base Class) - onkey[key]</h1>

<h1
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-onkey[key]-onkey[key]"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>onkey[key]</span></strong></h1>

<h2
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-onkey[key]-Description"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h2>

<p>Handler for when the key specified by [key] is pressed. Key handlers start
by checking on the current focused widget. If none are found, they will move up
the UI chain to any parent widgets.</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-layout=default
 data-local-id=330cfe44-7177-482a-8301-78cdad13595c>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>window.onkey2 = function() { util.debug('2'); };</pre><pre>window.onkey4 = function() { util.debug('4'); };</pre><pre>window.onkey6 = function() { util.debug('6'); };</pre><pre>window.onkey8 = function() { util.debug('8'); };</pre><pre>window.onkey* = digium.background;</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;</pre><pre>// all other keys would use this</pre><pre>window.onkey = function(evt) {</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;util.debug('one of my other keys');</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;util.debug(JSON.parse(evt)); //{&quot;key&quot; : &quot;keyname&quot;, &quot;type&quot; : &quot;key&quot; }</pre><pre>}</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><strong>onkey{dpad}</strong>: {dpad} can be (left, right, down,
up, select, cancel), corresponding to the 6 dpad buttons</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><strong>onkeyline{N}</strong>:&nbsp;{N} can be any line 2-6 that
your phone currently supports, which is up to 6 on a D70. Note: onkeyline1 is
reserved for closing the app (putting it into the background). For example,
onkeyline2 = function(){}</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><strong>onkey{N}</strong>: {N} can be 0-9 and corresponds to the
number pad. For example, onkey2 = function(){}</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><strong>onkey* or onkeystar</strong>: star / asterisk key on
number pad.</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><strong>onkey# or onkeypound</strong>: pound key on number pad.</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><strong>onkeyv{vol}</strong>: {vol} can be either up or down. For
example, onkeyvup&nbsp;= function(){}.</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><strong>onkey{function}</strong>: {function} can be any of the
various functional keys on your phone. Possibilites are as
follows:&nbsp;status, menu, dir, apps, info, conf, hdst, spkr, redial,hold,
msgs, xfer, and mute. Note: some of these are model dependent. For example,
onkeystatus = function(){}.</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><strong>onkeynum</strong>: This is a special catch all handler
for number keys. It is called if onkey[specific_number] doesn't exist but this
is set (any number key).</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><strong>onkey:</strong>&nbsp;This is a special catch all handler
for all keys.&nbsp;Any key press is called if the specific key doesn't exist
and if not onkeynum and it was a number key.</p>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Widget (Base Class) -
onsoftkey[key]</h1>

<h1
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-onsoftkey[key]-PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-onsoftkey[key]">Phone

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Widget (Base Class) -
setSoftkeyIcon</h1>

<h1
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-setSoftkeyIcon-PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-setSoftkeyIcon">Phone
API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Widget (Base Class) - setSoftkeyIcon</h1>

<h2
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-setSoftkeyIcon-setSoftkeyIcon"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>setSoftkeyIcon</span></strong></h2>

<h3
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-setSoftkeyIcon-Description"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h3>

<p>Sets an image object to display at the top left corner of the softkey.
Useful for indicating a hard key that calls the same handler. Suggested image
size is 5x5 pixels.</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-layout=default
 data-local-id=79c24a6a-e041-4dd3-b910-9f963fd80e19>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>&nbsp;exampleObj.setSoftkeyIcon(keyNum, icon);</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<p>If you require the app library, you can use Digium's set of softkey icons.
These image objects are created when the library is required.</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span>app.images.softKeys.left (left arrow)</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span>app.images.softKeys.right (right arrow)</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span>app.images.softKeys.up (up arrow)</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span>app.images.softKeys.down (down arrow)</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span>app.images.softKeys.select (check mark)</p>

<h3

<p>setSoftkeyIcon to set icons for the softkeys: Digium up arrow, Digium
checkmark, custom icon</p>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Widget (Base Class) -
setSoftkeysByList</h1>

<h1
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-setSoftkeysByList-PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-setSoftkeysByList">Phone
API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Widget (Base Class) - setSoftkeysByList</h1>

<h2
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-setSoftkeysByList-setSoftkeysByList"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>setSoftkeysByList</span></strong></h2>

<h3
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-setSoftkeysByList-Description"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h3>

<p>Sets up multiple softkeys at once. Assigning more than four softKeys causes
the fourth softkey to be a More softkey, which cycles the other three softkeys
through the list.</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-layout=default
 data-local-id=7423fd0d-9299-4b68-8a7e-8b3a6213335a>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>&nbsp;exampleObj.setSoftkeysByList( (Array)softKeys );</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<p>The argument&nbsp; <strong>softKeys&nbsp;</strong> that is&nbsp;passed into
the setSoftkeysByList method should be an array of parameters object as
described below. See the examples for more information.</p>

<h3
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-setSoftkeysByList-Parameters"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Parameters</span></strong></h3>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Widget (Base Class) -
takeFocus</h1>

<h1
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-takeFocus-PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-takeFocus">Phone
API Reference - UI Classes (Widgets) - Widget (Base Class) - takeFocus</h1>

<h2
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-takeFocus-takeFocus"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>takeFocus</span></strong></h2>

<h3
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-takeFocus-Description"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h3>

<p>Gives the selected widget keyboard focus. Calling this method triggers the
object's onFocus handler to be called, which must return true to take focus.</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-layout=default
 data-local-id=aa2f66cc-1c5c-4092-9865-23cdeabdaef4>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>&nbsp;exampleObject.takeFocus();</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<h3
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-takeFocus-Parameters"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Parameters</span></strong></h3>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-layout=default
 data-local-id=7fe554dd-c965-4c89-a2d7-4312fe348803>

  </td>
 </tr>

<h3
id="PhoneAPIReference-UIClasses(Widgets)-Widget(BaseClass)-takeFocus-Examples"><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Examples</span></strong></h3>

<p><strong>create a text object and give it keyboard focus</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-layout=default
 data-local-id=59eb80f1-1a54-4417-8f8a-545c8f8140ba>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>// the instantiation of the Text object could be replaced by any other Widget.</pre><pre>var textObject = new Text(0, 0, 100, 100, 'Test text for the widget.');</pre><pre>textObject.onFocus = function () {</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return true;</pre><pre>};</pre><pre>textObject.takeFocus();</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>

style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h3>

  data-theme=Confluence>textWidgetObj.h = (Text.LINE_HEIGHT * 2); //change the height of the Text object to 2x Line Height.</pre><pre>textWidgetObj.w = (textWidgetObj.w + 10); //add 10 to to current width of the Text object.</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Core</h1>

<div>

<div>

<p>Desk Phone API features described in this section are deprecated and
supported only on the following models: D40, d45, d50, d60, d62, d65, d70</p>

</div>

</div>

<p>These UI widgets are automatically instantiated for running apps. Apps
cannot create or destroy these widgets, and any UI elements that are to be
displayed must be added to them to be shown on the screen.</p>

<div>

  </td>
 </tr>

  <p>Any widgets added to digium.app.idleWindow will be displayed in the logo
  area of the phone's home screen.</p>

  through them at a rate defined by the&nbsp;idle_cycle_seconds&nbsp;setting in
  the phone's configuration.</p>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Core - digium.app.idleWindow</h1>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-UICore-digium.app.idleWindow-digium.app.idleWindow><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>digium.app.idleWindow</span></strong></h2>

<p>A specially instantiated Group widget displayed on the phone's idle screen
in place of the logo. This is only instantiated and available to the app after
the property 'hasIdle' has been set to true in its app.json file.</p>

<p>Any widgets added to digium.app.idleWindow will be displayed in the logo
area of the phone's home screen.</p>

<p>If multiple apps have provided idleWindow data, the phone will cycle through
them at a rate defined by the&nbsp;idle_cycle_seconds&nbsp;setting in the
phone's configuration.</p>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UICore-digium.app.idleWindow-Properties><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Properties</span></strong></h3>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=0f2aef5a-a39c-46bf-91c8-1c3055f42ece>
 <colgroup><col style="width: 133.0px;"><col style="width: 625.0px;"></colgroup>
 <tr>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p align=center style='text-align:center'><strong>Name&nbsp;</strong></p>
  </td>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-left:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p align=center style='text-align:center'><strong>Description&nbsp;</strong></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-top:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>hideBottomBar</p>
  </td>
  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>Boolean value that allows the app, when in control of the idleWindow,
  to&nbsp;<strong>hide the clock display area</strong>. This changes the height
  value of the idleWindow Group which allots more space for use.</p>
  <p><strong>Basic Example:</strong></p>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>digium.app.idleWindow.hideBottomBar = true;&nbsp;</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-top:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>hideTopBar</p>
  </td>
  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>Boolean value that allows the app, when in control of the idleWindow,
  to&nbsp;<strong>hide the presence status area</strong>&nbsp;(which displays
  Available, Do Not Disturb, etc.). This changes the height value of the
  idleWindow Group which allots more space for use.</p>
  <p><strong>Basic Example:</strong></p>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>&nbsp;digium.app.idleWindow.hideTopBar = true;</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Core - window</h1>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-UICore-window-window><strong><span style='font-family:
"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>window</span></strong></h2>

<p>Automatically instantiated Group widget available to each app.</p>

<p>The window object is the group that is displayed when the app is in the
foreground and its height and width proprerties are equal to the max for your
phone's model. It shares most of its methods and properties with the Group
widget. Adding other widgets to window will cause them to be displayed on the
screen when the app is in the foreground.</p>

<p>Any app that wishes to display something after being put in the foreground
must begin by attaching things to the window object.</p>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UICore-window-Methods><strong><span style='font-family:
"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Methods</span></strong></h3>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UICore-window-add-Examples><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Examples</span></strong></h3>

<p><strong>Using the 'add' method with a variety of widgets</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=63d989ab-5f55-4769-9a9a-79c230932cc4>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>

  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>&nbsp;// add a group to the window.</pre><pre>var group = new Group(0, 0, window.w, window.h);</pre><pre>window.add(group);</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;</pre><pre>//add a title to the group</pre><pre>group.add(new Text(0, 0, winow.w, Text.LINE_HEIGHT));</pre><pre>//add a scroll to the group slightly smaller due to the text @ top and offset the same.</pre><pre>var scroll = new Scroll(0, Text.LINE_HEIGHT, window.w, (window.h - Text.LINE_HEIGHT));</pre><pre>group.add(list);</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;</pre><pre>//add a set of images to the list.</pre><pre>var img1 = new Image(&quot;tmp&quot;, &quot;test1.png&quot;, 30, 30, 50, 10);</pre><pre>var img2 = new Image(&quot;tmp&quot;, &quot;test2.png&quot;, 30, 45, 50, 10)</pre><pre>var img3 = new Image(&quot;tmp&quot;, &quot;test3.png&quot;, 30, 60, 50, 10)</pre><pre>scroll.add(img1, img2, img3); //support for adding multiple is the same with group and window.</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Core - window - clear</h1>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UICore-window-clear-Description><strong><span

list.</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760

  data-theme=Confluence>&nbsp;exampleObj.clear();</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UICore-window-clear-Parameters><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Parameters</span></strong></h3>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=d8abec3b-cddf-4d9d-a17b-e35d91973b7e>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>None</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended</h1>

<div>

<div>

<p>Desk Phone API features described in this section are deprecated and
supported only on the following models: D40, d45, d50, d60, d62, d65, d70</p>

</div>

</div>

<p>These extended UI libraries provide additional UI functionality and methods
and are available if required. They provide more advanced UI functions and act
as a shortcut to commonly invoked design patterns (e.g., creating a form
composed of labels and inputs). The functionality provided by these libraries
could be recreated by any app using the base UI components.</p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=988
 data-layout=default data-local-id=c3cb71ee-03d1-4c3f-9582-4380734c59ec>
 <colgroup><col style="width: 132.0px;"><col style="width: 856.0px;"></colgroup>
 <tr>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p align=center style='text-align:center'><strong>Name&nbsp;</strong></p>
  </td>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-left:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p align=center style='text-align:center'><strong>Description&nbsp;</strong></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-top:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p><a
  href="/wiki/spaces/Phones/pages/23429394/Phone+API+Reference+-+UI+Extended+-+screen"
  data-linked-resource-id=23429394 data-linked-resource-version=3
  data-linked-resource-type=page>screen</a></p>
  </td>
  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>Library containing a set of functions to aid with building a standard UI.</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-top:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p><a
  href="/wiki/spaces/Phones/pages/22119003/Phone+API+Reference+-+UI+Extended+-+genericForm"
  data-linked-resource-id=22119003 data-linked-resource-version=3
  data-linked-resource-type=page>genericForm</a></p>
  </td>
  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>Creates a form containing various input objects. Can be used to display a
  settings page for an app, for example. This is a useful shortcut for creating
  a page with many elements, without having to manually define and position
  each element.</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-top:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>

  href="/wiki/spaces/Phones/pages/22675759/Phone+API+Reference+-+UI+Extended+-+genericMenu"
  data-linked-resource-id=22675759 data-linked-resource-version=3
  data-linked-resource-type=page>genericMenu</a></p>
  </td>
  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>Displays a menu to the user. A list of key handlers/softkeys for each menu
  item can be specified.&nbsp;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-top:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>

  </td>
 </tr>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended - genericConfirm.show</h1>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-genericConfirm.show-genericConfirm.show><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>genericConfirm.show</span></strong></h2>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-genericConfirm.show-Description><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h3>

<p>Displays a confirmation prompt to the user. All widgets currently on screen
are hidden while the user is prompted for a choice. When the user makes a
choice, the widgets are shown again, and a callback is executed with the user's
choice passed as a parameter.</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=af260072-0ffb-422f-835e-d8c4c208143e>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>genericConfirm.show(parameters);</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Parameters</span></strong></h3>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-genericConfirm.show-Examples><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Examples</span></strong></h3>

<p><strong>genericConfirm prompts user to continue</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=eb4a237d-b468-4882-941d-cae55dc33906>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>var genericConfirm = require('genericConfirm');</pre><pre>this.processConfirm = function (params) {</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;if (params.confirm === true) {</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;continue();</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} else {</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;digium.background();</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</pre><pre>};</pre><pre>genericConfirm.show({</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'id'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'confirm_1',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'message'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'Would you like to continue?',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'title'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'Confirm',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'object'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : this,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'confirmBtnText'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'Continue',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'hideCancelButton'&nbsp; : false,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'cancelBtnText'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'Cancel',</pre><pre>});</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended - genericForm</h1>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-genericForm-genericForm><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>genericForm</span></strong></h2>

<p>Creates a form containing various input objects. Can be used to display a
settings page for an app, for example. This is a useful shortcut for creating a
page with many elements, without having to manually define and position each
element.</p>

<p><strong>Require Extended Library:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=fd5cf576-5893-406b-b353-02e0661d217b>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>var genericForm = require('genericForm');</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;

  <p>false</p>
  </td>
  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>Whether or not to execute the onchange callback (if one exists) for the
  input.</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-genericForm.setValue-Examples><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Examples</span></strong></h3>

<p>genericForm.setValue to set the value of the input</p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0

 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'

  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>//in the example below, this fills the 'sample_normalInput' textbox with the string 'Foo Bar'</pre><pre>//the onchange event is not executed</pre><pre>genericForm.setValue({</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'setting'&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'sample_normalInput',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'value'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'Foo Bar',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'skipOnChange'&nbsp; : true</pre><pre>});</pre></div>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended - genericForm.show</h1>

<h1
id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-genericForm.show-PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-genericForm.show>Phone
API Reference - UI Extended - genericForm.show</h1>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-genericForm.show-genericForm.show><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>genericForm.show</span></strong></h2>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-genericForm.show-Description><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h3>

<p>Clears anything currently on the screen and shows the form.</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-layout=default
 data-local-id=bba290e7-a670-4a45-abce-d5131e3d41fd>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>&nbsp;genericForm.show(parameters);</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<p>List of genericForm inputTypes:</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><strong>normal</strong>: Basic Input UI Widget</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><strong>textCycler</strong>: TextCycler Extended Class</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><strong>selectInput</strong>: SelectInput Extended Class</p>

<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><strong>hostInput</strong>: Group of inputs that all input
hostname or ip address</p>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-genericForm.show-Examples><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Examples</span></strong></h3>

<p><strong>genericForm.show containing each of the possible input types can be
created as follows:</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-layout=default
 data-local-id=3e23c79f-d271-4e9d-b1c0-2dae18578193>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>var app = require('app');</pre><pre>app.init();</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;</pre><pre>var genericForm = require('genericForm');</pre><pre>//The array of input items to use in the form</pre><pre>var items = [</pre><pre>{</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'text'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'sample TextCycler',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'setting'&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'sample_textCycler',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'inputType' : 'textCycler',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'inputParams'&nbsp;&nbsp; : {</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'options'&nbsp;&nbsp; : [</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{'display' : 'textCycler1', 'value' : 1},</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{'display' : 'textCycler2', 'value' : 2}</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;]&nbsp;&nbsp;</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</pre><pre>},</pre><pre>{</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'text'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'sample hostInput',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'setting'&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'sample_hostInput',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'inputType' : 'hostInput',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'inputParams'&nbsp;&nbsp; : {</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'showDotSoftkey'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : true,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'allowInputTypeChange'&nbsp; : true</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</pre><pre>},</pre><pre>{</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'text'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'sample selectInput',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'setting'&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'sample_selectInput',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'inputType' : 'selectInput',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'inputParams'&nbsp;&nbsp; : {</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'title'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'sample title',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'softkeyLabel'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'softkey',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'softkeyCallback'&nbsp;&nbsp; : function () { }, //callback goes here</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'options'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : [</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{'display' : 'selectInput1', 'value' : 1},</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{'display' : 'selectInput2', 'value' : 2}</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;]&nbsp;&nbsp;</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</pre><pre>},</pre><pre>{</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'text'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'sample normalInput',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'setting'&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'sample_normalInput',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'inputType' : 'normal',&nbsp; //'numeric' inputType makes a similar input widget</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'validate'&nbsp; : '[a-z]+[0-9]+', //require at least one letter followed by at least one digit</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'errorMsg'&nbsp; : 'normalInput must contain a letter followed by a number',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'inputParams'&nbsp;&nbsp; : {}</pre><pre>},</pre><pre>{</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'text'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'sample text',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'setting'&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'sample_text',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'inputType' : 'text',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'inputParams'&nbsp;&nbsp; : {}</pre><pre>}</pre><pre>];</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;</pre><pre>//The form is constructed and shown:</pre><pre>genericForm.show({</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'id'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'exampleForm',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'labelWidth'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : (digium.phoneModel === 'D70') ? 140 : 125,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'values'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : {</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'sample_textCycler' : 1,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'sample_hostInput'&nbsp; : '192.168.1.1',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'sample_selectInput'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 2,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'sample_normalInput'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'Some Text',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'sample_text'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'This is a text input'</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;},</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'inputs'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : items,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'object'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : this,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'title'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'Sample Form',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'onkeyline1'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : digium.background,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'onkeycancel'&nbsp;&nbsp; : digium.background,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'forceRedraw'&nbsp;&nbsp; : true</pre><pre>});</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;</p>

</div>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended - genericMenu</h1>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-genericMenu-genericMenu><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>genericMenu</span></strong></h2>

<p>Displays a menu to the user. A list of key handlers/softkeys for each menu
item can be specified.&nbsp;</p>

  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"

 </tr>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended - genericMenu.show</h1>

pressing a number pad key to jump to that menu item.</p>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-genericMenu.show-Examples><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Examples</span></strong></h3>

<p><strong>genericMenu.show creates a menu</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=26162ee8-be01-4596-ba48-4e4610b0fc24>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>var genericMenu = require('genericMenu');</pre><pre>var handler = {};</pre><pre>//This handler is called when any assigned softkeys/hardkeys are pressed</pre><pre>//It receives the id of the selected item and the action as parameters</pre><pre>handler.processMenuAction = function (params) {</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;switch (params.actionId) {</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;case 'select':</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;selectCallback(params.selectionId);</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;break;</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;case 'help':</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;helpCallback(params.selectionId);</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;break;</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;case 'getInfo':</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;getInfo(params.selectionId);</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;break;</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;case 'exit':</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;digium.background();</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;break;</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</pre><pre>};</pre><pre>//the menu items are defined in an array</pre><pre>var items = [</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'text'&nbsp; : 'Menu Entry 1',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'id'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'item_1'</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;},</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'text'&nbsp; : 'Menu Entry 2',&nbsp;&nbsp;</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'id'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'item_2'</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;},</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'text'&nbsp; : 'Menu Entry 3',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'id'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'item_3'</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;},</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'text'&nbsp; : 'Menu Entry 4',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'id'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'item_4'</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</pre><pre>];</pre><pre>//the softkeys are defined in an array</pre><pre>var softkeys = [</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'label'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'Select',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'actionId'&nbsp; : 'select',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'icon'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : app.images.softKeys.select</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;},</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'label'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'Help',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'actionId'&nbsp; : 'help'</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;},</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'label'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'Info',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'actionId'&nbsp; : 'getInfo'</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;},</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'label'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'Cancel',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'actionId'&nbsp; : 'exit'</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</pre><pre>];</pre><pre>//show the menu</pre><pre>genericMenu.show({</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'id'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'menu_1',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'menu'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : items,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'object'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : handler,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'title'&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : 'Menu Title',</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'softkeys'&nbsp; : softkeys,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'onkeyselect'&nbsp;&nbsp; : selectCallback,</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'onkeycancel'&nbsp;&nbsp; : digium.background</pre><pre>});</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended - genericMenu.takeFocus</h1>

<h2
id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-genericMenu.takeFocus-genericMenu.takeFocus><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>genericMenu.takeFocus</span></strong></h2>

<div>

 </tr>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended - screen.setTitleText</h1>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-screen.setTitleText-screen.setTitleText><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>screen.setTitleText</span></strong></h2>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtended-screen.setTitleText-Description><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h3>

<p>Returns a textWidget that can be added to the window. To be used as the
title bar at the top of the screen. The title is displayed in white text on a
black background one text line high. This is useful mostly if you want to make
your apps look and feel similar to the factory Digium apps.</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:</strong>&nbsp;</p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=fb70e56a-7838-4ef6-8429-08aa3c5df9fe>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>&nbsp;screen.setTitleText(parameters);</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0

  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>var screen = require('screen'); //require our extended library</pre><pre>window.clear(); //clear the screen</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;</pre><pre>var titleW = screen.setTitleText({'title' : 'title'}); //call our method to make a title widget</pre><pre>window.add(titleW); //add it to the screen</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<p><strong>Widget from setTitleText added to window</strong><br>
This is from the example. A simple titleText was added to window. the
&quot;titleText&quot; refers to just the black bar and text across the top.</p>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended Classes</h1>

<div>

<div>

<p>Desk Phone API features described in this section are deprecated and
supported only on the following models: D40, d45, d50, d60, d62, d65, d70</p>

</div>

</div>

<p>These objects provide UI functionality and are available to apps that
require specific libraries. They provide more advanced UI functions and act as
a shortcut to commonly invoked design patterns (e.g., displaying a menu of
options to the user). The functionality provided by these libraries could be
recreated by any app using the base UI components.</p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=988
 data-layout=default data-local-id=2e5249fe-0cdf-4626-bcc7-32425f7c382a>
 <colgroup><col style="width: 96.0px;"><col style="width: 892.0px;"></colgroup>
 <tr>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p align=center style='text-align:center'><strong>Name&nbsp;</strong></p>
  </td>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-left:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p align=center style='text-align:center'><strong>Description&nbsp;</strong></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-top:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p><a
  href="/wiki/spaces/Phones/pages/23429505/Phone+API+Reference+-+UI+Extended+Classes+-+SelectInput"
  data-linked-resource-id=23429505 data-linked-resource-version=3
  data-linked-resource-type=page>SelectInput</a></p>
  </td>
  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>Combines a variety of core objects to create a simple control that is
  analgous to a web browser's select input (dropdown). Allows the user to open
  a new screen and scroll through a list of options. Recommended for large
  lists.</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-top:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p><a
  href="/wiki/spaces/Phones/pages/23462180/Phone+API+Reference+-+UI+Extended+Classes+-+TextCycler"
  data-linked-resource-id=23462180 data-linked-resource-version=3
  data-linked-resource-type=page>TextCycler</a></p>
  </td>
  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>Combines a variety of core objects to create a simple control that is
  analgous to a web browser's radio group. Allows you to present a list of
  options for input. Recommended for lists with fewer than 10 options.</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;</p>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended Classes - SelectInput</h1>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtendedClasses-SelectInput-SelectInput><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>SelectInput</span></strong></h2>

<p>Combines a variety of core objects to create a simple control that is
analgous to a web browser's select input (dropdown). Allows the user to open a
new screen and scroll through a list of options. Recommended for large lists.</p>

<p><strong>Require Extended Library:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=ecff150b-079c-4578-aa37-2b704915ddd2>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>var app = require('app');</pre><pre>app.init(); //app must be required and initialized somewhere before creating SelectInputs</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;</pre><pre>require('SelectInput').SelectInput;</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtendedClasses-SelectInput-ClassConstructor><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Class Constructor</span></strong></h3>

SelectInput()</u></h4>

<p>This extended class is not a child of base widget, so it cannot be added
directly to the screen. Access the textWidget property to add or remove it from
the screen. This extended class requires the&nbsp; <a
href="https://wiki-legacy.freepbx.org/display/PHON/Phone+API+Reference+-+Extended+-+app">'app'
library</a> ,&nbsp;and it must be initialized with an init function.&nbsp;</p>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended Classes - SelectInput - setValue</h1>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtendedClasses-SelectInput-setValue-setValue><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>setValue</span></strong></h2>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtendedClasses-SelectInput-setValue-Description><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h3>

<p>Sets the value of the object to one of the possible options</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended Classes - SelectInput - takeFocus</h1>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtendedClasses-SelectInput-takeFocus-takeFocus><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>takeFocus</span></strong></h2>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtendedClasses-SelectInput-takeFocus-Description><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h3>

<p>Gives the selected widget keyboard focus. Calling this method triggers the
object's onFocus handler to be called, which must return true to take focus.</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=20cc1132-7786-4b4c-91e5-413bbbe12336>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>exampleObject.takeFocus();</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtendedClasses-SelectInput-takeFocus-Parameters><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Parameters</span></strong></h3>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=2bec579c-b74c-4075-8d3c-60afeb68ec96>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>None</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtendedClasses-SelectInput-takeFocus-Examples><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Examples</span></strong></h3>

<p><strong>create a text object and give it keyboard focus</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=02bac746-7d74-46c4-bca2-01e266dd9cd2>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>// the instantiation of the Text object could be replaced by any other Widget.</pre><pre>var textObject = new Text(0, 0, 100, 100, 'Test text for the widget.');</pre><pre>textObject.onFocus = function () {</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return true;</pre><pre>};</pre><pre>textObject.takeFocus();</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended Classes - TextCycler</h1>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtendedClasses-TextCycler-TextCycler><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>TextCycler</span></strong></h2>

<p>Combines a variety of core objects to create a simple control that is
analgous to a web browser's radio group. Allows you to present a list of
options for input. Recommended for lists with fewer than 10 options.</p>

<p><strong>Require Extended Library:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760
 data-layout=default data-local-id=45985237-457d-4dac-a852-21c0de946429>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>var app = require('app');</pre><pre>app.init(); //app must be required and initialized somewhere before creating TextCyclers</pre><pre>&nbsp;&nbsp;</pre><pre>require('TextCycler').TextCycler;</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtendedClasses-TextCycler-ClassConstructor><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Class Constructor</span></strong></h3>

TextCycler</u></h4>

</div>

<p>This extended class is not a child of base widget, so it cannot be added
directly to the screen. Access the textWidget property to add or remove it from
the screen. This extended class requires the&nbsp; <a
href="https://wiki-legacy.freepbx.org/display/PHON/Phone+API+Reference+-+Extended+-+app">'app'
library</a> ,&nbsp;and it must be initialized with an init function.&nbsp;</p>

  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>Sets the value of the object to one of the possible options</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-top:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p><a
  href="/wiki/spaces/Phones/pages/24018952/Phone+API+Reference+-+UI+Extended+Classes+-+TextCycler+-+takeFocus"
  data-linked-resource-id=24018952 data-linked-resource-version=2
  data-linked-resource-type=page>takeFocus</a></p>
  </td>
  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>Gives the selected widget keyboard focus. Calling this method triggers the
  object's onFocus handler to be called, which must return true to take focus.</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<h1>Phone API Reference - UI Extended Classes - TextCycler - takeFocus</h1>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtendedClasses-TextCycler-takeFocus-takeFocus><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>takeFocus</span></strong></h2>

<h3 id=PhoneAPIReference-UIExtendedClasses-TextCycler-takeFocus-Description><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h3>

<p>Gives the selected widget keyboard focus. Calling this method triggers the
object's onFocus handler to be called, which must return true to take focus.</p>

<p><strong>Basic Example:&nbsp;</strong></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=760

 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour=initial>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>exampleObject.takeFocus();</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

style='font-family:"Aptos",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Parameters</span></strong></h3>

<h1>Phone API Reference -Extended - app.showErrors</h1>

<h1
id=PhoneAPIReference-Extended-app.showErrors-PhoneAPIReference-Extended-app.showErrors><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Phone API
Reference -Extended - app.showErrors</span></strong></h1>

<h1 id=PhoneAPIReference-Extended-app.showErrors-app.showErrors><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>app.showErrors</span></strong></h1>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-Extended-app.showErrors-Description><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Description</span></strong></h2>

<p>Clears the screen and shows an error popup on the entire screen. Takes an
array of error messages so you can show multiple messages at one time.</p>

<p>Basic Example:&nbsp;</p>

<div>

<div><pre
data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
data-theme=Confluence>app.showErrors(parameters);</pre></div>

</div>

<p>The errors array should contain at least one object that requires the key
'message.' In addition, 'code' can be used to supply an error code in parens at
the end of the message.</p>

<h2 id=PhoneAPIReference-Extended-app.showErrors-Parameters><strong><span
style='font-family:"Aptos Display",sans-serif;font-weight:normal'>Parameters</span></strong></h2>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none' data-table-width=1068
 data-layout=default data-local-id=af50a459-7fb2-4f96-bbec-c6ffcc5c80fb>
 <colgroup><col style="width: 181.0px;"><col style="width: 88.0px;"><col style="width: 84.0px;"><col style="width: 105.0px;"><col style="width: 610.0px;"></colgroup>
 <tr style='page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour="#f4f5f7">
  <p align=center style='text-align:center'><strong>Name</strong></p>
  </td>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-left:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour="#f4f5f7">
  <p align=center style='text-align:center'><strong>Required</strong></p>
  </td>
  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-left:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'
  data-highlight-colour="#f4f5f7">
  <p align=center style='text-align:center'><strong>Type</strong></p>
  </td>

  data-highlight-colour="#f4f5f7">

  </td>

  data-highlight-colour="#f4f5f7">
  <p align=center style='text-align:center'><strong>Description</strong></p>
  </td>
 </tr>

  <td style='border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-top:none;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>errors (app.showErrors)</p>

  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>Yes</p>
  </td>
  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>array</p>
  </td>
  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'></td>
  <td style='border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt 3.75pt'>
  <p>An array of messages for display. Each item in the array should be an
  object that requires the key 'message' and can optionally take the key
  'code.'</p>
  <div>
  <div><pre
  data-syntaxhighlighter-params="brush: java; gutter: false; theme: Confluence"
  data-theme=Confluence>[{</pre><pre>    'message' : 'Bad Number',</pre><pre>    'code'    : '123313'</pre><pre>}, {</pre><pre>    'message' : 'Too short'</pre><pre>}];</pre></div>
  </div>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<br>
<strong>An example Error Screen</strong><br>
This error screen is a result of the app.checkRequired function. If you
manually form your on errors array, it will look the same.&nbsp;</p>

<h1>Sangoma Phone App Engine</h1>

<div>

<div>

<p>Desk Phone API features described in this section are deprecated and
supported only on the following models: D40, d45, d50, d60, d62, d65, d70</p>

</div>

</div>

<p class=MsoNormal><img border=0 width=240 height=120 id="Picture 1187675007"
src="Digium%20One%20Page_files/image014.png"></p>

<p>The Sangoma Phone API&nbsp;lets you build custom apps for your phones using
the popular programming language&nbsp;<strong>JavaScript.&nbsp;</strong>And&nbsp;the
Sangoma Phone App Engine interprets and executes this JavaScript code.</p>

<p>If you have done any web development, you have probably dabbled in
JavaScript. If so, you're already halfway there in learning how to write a
custom app for your Sangoma Phones.&nbsp;</p>

<p>If you haven't been exposed to JavaScript, visit the&nbsp;<a
href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/JavaScript">discussion of
JavaScript</a>&nbsp;on the Mozilla Developer Network for a good introduction
and plenty of references for learning JavaScript.</p>

<p>Note: The Sangoma Phone App Engine is based on the Chrome V8 Engine, which
supports all ECMAScript 5 standards.&nbsp;</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;</p>

</div>

</body>

</html>
